WELCOME TO
ACADEMY OF TECHNOLOGY
| ABOUT
SPDY :
Established in 2007, Academy of Technology is one of the most acclaimed self-financed engineering colleges in Karnataka. It has been established by SPDY Educational Development & Charitable Organisation (SPDYEDCO),
a trust known for its deep sense of social commitment and dedicated to the promotion of education by inculcating appropriate ethics and attitude.
In a metamorphosis of over 18 years, Academy of Technology has been reinventing itself constantly to explore the infinite possibilities of engineering and technology – an academy that inspires everyone to think differently. It is now the preferred career destination for meritorious students due to its academic integrity and standard as well as its attractive campus placement.
| UPCOMING
EVENTS :
| HIGHLIGHTS

| DEPARTMENTS

| FAQ
:
What is the total fee payable at the time of admission for regular students?
The total fee payable at the time of admission for regular students is ₹1,05,200.
What is the total fee payable at the time of admission for students allotted through TFW (Tuition Fee Waiver) scheme?
The total fee payable at the time of admission for students allotted through TFW is ₹53,200.
How much is the tuition fee per semester?
The tuition fee per semester is ₹52,000.
Are there any additional fees that might be charged by the University (MAKAUT)?
Yes, there are additional fees charged by the University, which include:  1) University Development Fees @ ₹550 per year (one-time payment of ₹2,200) 2) University Registration Fees @ ₹500 (one-time payment)
Is the caution deposit refundable?
Yes, the caution deposit of ₹10,000 is refundable.
How can the fees be paid?
The fees can be paid by cash or demand draft in favour of 'ACADEMY OF TECHNOLOGY,' payable at Kolkata.
Are the tuition fees subject to change?
Yes, the tuition fees may be revised based on directives from the West Bengal Government.
What is the Vidyarthi Mediclaim, and how much does it cost?
Vidyarthi Mediclaim is a medical insurance for students, and it costs ₹2,500 (one-time payment).
What are the fees for library services?
The library fees, which cover the Book Bank, Journals, and Digital Library, amount to ₹6,000 (one-time payment).

WELCOME TO
ACADEMY OF TECHNOLOGY
“Aspires to be a pre-eminent deemed university of national standing in education and innovation”.
All academic programmes are approved by AICTE, recognized by Department of Higher Education, Government of West Bengal and affiliated to Maulana Abul Kalam Azad University of Technology, West Bengal (formerly West Bengal University of Technology) .
| ABOUT
SPDY :
Established in 2007, Academy of Technology is one of the most acclaimed self-financed engineering colleges in Karnataka. It has been established by SPDY Educational Development & Charitable Organisation (SPDYEDCO),
a trust known for its deep sense of social commitment and dedicated to the promotion of education by inculcating appropriate ethics and attitude.
In a metamorphosis of over 18 years, Academy of Technology has been reinventing itself constantly to explore the infinite possibilities of engineering and technology – an academy that inspires everyone to think differently. It is now the preferred career destination for meritorious students due to its academic integrity and standard as well as its attractive campus placement.
